11._CD Modeling_NN procedure_NN for_IN solving_VVG the_DT wave-vessel_NP impact_NN problem_NN ._SENT 
4.1_CD ._SENT 
Non-linear_JJ free_JJ surface_NN modeling_VVG Different_JJ numerical_JJ methods_NNS have_VHP been_VBN developed_VVN to_TO address_VV discontinuities_NNS ._SENT 
Lagrangian_JJ and_CC Eulerian_JJ approaches_NNS have_VHP been_VBN used_VVN in_IN successful_JJ numerical_JJ approaches_NNS to_TO approximate_JJ free_JJ boundaries_NNS in_IN fluid_JJ flow_NN ._SENT

Several_JJ reviews_NNS of_IN free_JJ surface_NN flow_NN are_VBP available_JJ by_IN Mei_NNS (_( 1978_CD )_) ,_, for_IN linear_JJ free_JJ surface_NN flow_NN using_VVG integral_JJ methods_NNS ;_: Floryan_NP and_CC Rasmussen_NP (_( 1989_CD )_) ,_, for_IN numerical_JJ methods_NNS for_IN viscous_JJ flows_NNS with_IN moving_VVG interfaces_NNS ;_: and_CC Tsai_NP and_CC Yue_NP (_( 1996_CD )_) for_IN computational_JJ methods_NNS of_IN non-linear_JJ free_JJ surface_NN flows_NNS ._SENT 
4.1.1_CD ._SENT 
Marker_NN and_CC cell_NN (_( MAC_NN )_) Harlow_NP and_CC Welch_NP (_( 1965_CD )_) introduced_VVD the_DT MAC_NN method_NN for_IN simulating_VVG free_JJ surface_NN flow_NN which_WDT is_VBZ a_DT development_NN on_IN the_DT previous_JJ Particle-in-cell_NN (_( PIC_NP )_) code_NN ._SENT 
PIC_JJ used_JJ mass_NN particles_NNS that_WDT carried_VVD position_NN ,_, mass_NN ,_, and_CC species_NN information_NN (_( Evans_NP and_CC Harlow_NP ,_, 1957_CD ,_, Harlow_NP ,_, 1965_CD )_) ._SENT 
The_DT MAC_NN method_NN is_VBZ a_DT finite_JJ difference_NN technique_NN on_IN a_DT staggered_JJ grid_NN for_IN solving_VVG incompressible_JJ viscous_JJ free_JJ surface_NN flow_NN and_CC employs_VVZ variables_NNS of_IN pressure_NN and_CC velocity_NN as_IN the_DT primary_JJ dependent_JJ variables_NNS ._SENT 
The_DT MAC_NN method_NN defines_VVZ whether_IN a_DT cell_NN contains_VVZ fluid_JJ or_CC not_RB (_( McKee_NP et_NP al_NP ._SENT 
,_, 2008_CD )_) ._SENT 
The_DT cell_NN contains_VVZ a_DT particle_NN it_PP is_VBZ labelled_VVN “contains_NP fluid”_NP ,_, and_CC if_IN not_RB ,_, it_PP is_VBZ labelled_VVN “empty”_NP (_( Harlow_NP et_NP al_NP ._SENT 
,_, 1976_CD )_) ._SENT 
This_DT means_VVZ that_IN marker_NN particles_NNS can_MD cover_VV the_DT whole_JJ fluid_JJ area_NN while_IN each_DT specific_JJ particle_NN moves_NNS with_IN the_DT fluid_JJ velocity_NN in_IN its_PP$ own_JJ coordinates_VVZ ._SENT 
Storage_NN requirements_NNS for_IN this_DT method_NN increase_NN significantly_RB because_IN of_IN the_DT number_NN of_IN point_NN locations_NNS that_WDT must_MD be_VB stored_VVN ._SENT 
Amsden_NP and_CC Harlow_NP (_( 1970_CD )_) introduced_VVD a_DT new_JJ simplified_VVN version_NN of_IN MAC_NN which_WDT is_VBZ called_VVN SMAC_NN ._SENT 
It_PP reduces_VVZ the_DT difficulties_NNS of_IN the_DT first_JJ version_NN by_IN splitting_NN the_DT calculation_NN into_IN two_CD parts_NNS in_IN the_DT ZUNI_NP code_NN ._SENT 
Current_JJ MAC_NN methods_NNS incorporate_VV the_DT ability_NN to_TO follow_VV the_DT free_JJ surface_NN ,_, and_CC they_PP are_VBP able_JJ to_TO calculate_VV separation_NN ._SENT 
The_DT MAC_NN method_NN was_VBD the_DT base_NN of_IN the_DT creation_NN of_IN other_JJ advanced_JJ methods_NNS which_WDT are_VBP particle-less_JJ and_CC based_VVN on_IN the_DT implicit_JJ scheme_NN such_JJ as_IN the_DT implicit-fluid_NP Eulerian_NP (_( ICE_NN )_) method_NN (_( Harlow_NP and_CC Welch_NP ,_, 1981_CD )_) ._SENT 
Before_IN the_DT appearance_NN of_IN the_DT MAC_NN method_NN ,_, Francis_NP Harlow_NP in_IN the_DT 1960s_NNS created_VVD a_DT particle-in-cell_NN (_( PIC_NP )_) method_NN (_( Evans_NP and_CC Harlow_NP ,_, 1957_CD ,_, Harlow_NP ,_, 1965_CD )_) ,_, which_WDT uses_VVZ mass_NN particles_NNS and_CC includes_VVZ material_NN position_NN and_CC mass_NN information_NN ._SENT 
This_DT method_NN has_VHZ a_DT special_JJ capability_NN to_TO numerically_RB model_JJ flow_NN ,_, which_WDT has_VHZ large_JJ distortion_NN and_CC compressions_NNS in_IN several_JJ spatial_JJ dimensions_NNS ._SENT 
In_IN this_DT method_NN a_DT single_JJ fluid_NN tracked_VVN in_IN the_DT continuous_JJ phase_NN uses_VVZ the_DT Lagrangian_JJ approach_NN ,_, while_IN densities_NNS and_CC currents_NNS are_VBP calculated_VVN with_IN the_DT Eulerian_JJ approach_NN (_( Evans_NP et_NP al_NP ._SENT 
,_, 1957_CD )_) ._SENT 
This_DT method_NN does_VVZ not_RB give_VV an_DT accurate_JJ solution_NN because_IN of_IN numerical_JJ diffusion_NN and_CC is_VBZ noisy_JJ ._SENT 
The_DT difficulties_NNS of_IN this_DT method_NN are_VBP well-documented_VVN ._SENT 
To_TO make_VV the_DT PIC_NP method_NN as_IN accurate_JJ as_IN other_JJ methods_NNS ,_, the_DT viscosity_NN and_CC heat_NN conduction_NN calculation_NN must_MD be_VB reduced_VVN ._SENT 
Brackbill_NP ,_, 1988_CD ,_, Brackbill_NP ,_, 1991_CD introduced_VVD a_DT new_JJ model_NN entitled_VVN Fluid_JJ Implicit_JJ Particle_NN method_NN (_( FLIP_JJ )_) which_WDT overcame_VVD the_DT problem_NN of_IN numerical_JJ diffusion_NN using_VVG fully_RB Lagrangian_JJ particles_NNS ._SENT 
4.1.2_CD ._SENT 
Volume_NN of_IN fluid_JJ (_( VOF_NP )_) Hirt_NP and_CC Nichols_NP (_( 1981_CD )_) first_RB introduced_VVD the_DT VOF_JJ method_NN which_WDT was_VBD simple_JJ and_CC efficient_JJ compared_VVN to_TO other_JJ models_NNS for_IN the_DT calculation_NN of_IN free_JJ boundaries_NNS ._SENT 
This_DT Eulerian_JJ technique_NN was_VBD used_VVN to_TO numerically_RB simulate_VVP deformation_NN of_IN a_DT free_JJ surface_NN ._SENT 
VOF_NP defines_VVZ a_DT fluid_JJ fraction_NN function_NN F(x_NP ,_, y_NP ,_, t_NN )_) ,_, which_WDT has_VHZ a_DT value_NN between_IN unity_NN and_CC zero_CD which_WDT represents_VVZ the_DT volume_NN fraction_NN of_IN the_DT cell_NN occupied_VVN by_IN fluid_NN ._SENT 
Cells_NNS with_IN F_NN value_NN between_IN zero_CD and_CC one_CD represent_VVP a_DT free_JJ surface_NN and_CC they_PP must_MD have_VH at_IN least_JJS one_CD neighbouring_VVG cell_NN for_IN which_WDT the_DT F_NN value_NN equals_VVZ zero_CD ._SENT 
The_DT VOF_JJ method_NN requires_VVZ less_JJR storage_NN capacity_NN for_IN each_DT cell_NN ._SENT 
The_DT derivative_NN of_IN F_NN can_MD be_VB used_VVN to_TO calculate_VV the_DT boundary_NN normal_JJ ._SENT

Sprinkler_NN atomizer_NN A_DT sprinkler_NN jet_NN ,_, which_WDT is_VBZ particularly_RB used_VVN for_IN distributing_VVG water_NN droplets_NNS works_NNS based_VVN on_IN sheet_NN and_CC droplet_NN breakup_NN ._SENT

(_( 2007_CD )_) developed_VVD a_DT physics-based_JJ atomization_NN model_NN for_IN predicting_VVG the_DT spray_NN using_VVG a_DT free_JJ surface_NN boundary_NN layer_NN and_CC dispersion_NN theories_NNS ._SENT

The_DT sheet_NN breakup_NN was_VBD investigated_VVN and_CC the_DT governing_VVG equations_NNS were_VBD developed_VVN ._SENT

,_, 2007_CD )_) ._SENT

<Section> 6._CD Conclusion_NN </Section> The_DT focus_NN of_IN this_DT review_NN is_VBZ on_IN the_DT direct_JJ and_CC related_JJ topics_NNS to_TO spray_NN cloud_NN covering_VVG the_DT complex_JJ process_NN ,_, such_JJ as_IN wave_NN slamming_VVG ,_, free_JJ surface_NN modeling_NN ,_, air_NN entrainment_NN ,_, and_CC sheet_NN breakup_NN ._SENT 
In_IN the_DT first_JJ section_NN ,_, existing_VVG field_NN observations_NNS involved_VVN in_IN the_DT study_NN of_IN the_DT LWC_NN and_CC spray_NN height_NN are_VBP reviewed_VVN ._SENT 
This_DT shows_VVZ a_DT need_NN for_IN more_JJR observations_NNS with_IN better_JJR and_CC accurate_JJ measurements_NNS of_IN the_DT variables_NNS of_IN spray_NN clouds_NNS ,_, such_JJ as_IN droplet_NN velocities_NNS ,_, sizes_NNS ,_, and_CC locations_NNS ._SENT 
Full_JJ scale_NN measurements_NNS are_VBP useful_JJ in_IN studying_VVG the_DT process_NN ._SENT 
Early_JJ measurements_NNS illustrated_VVD the_DT importance_NN of_IN spray_NN cloud_NN formation_NN ,_, but_CC these_DT measured_VVN data_NNS were_VBD not_RB sufficiently_RB detailed_JJ to_TO be_VB used_VVN to_TO validate_VV the_DT computational_JJ results_NNS or_CC lab_NN scale_NN experimental_JJ data_NNS ._SENT 
Section_NN two_CD covers_VVZ numerical_JJ and_CC experimental_JJ studies_NNS of_IN wave-ship_NN impact_NN ._SENT 
Studies_NNS directly_RB related_VVN to_TO modeling_VVG the_DT spray_NN cloud_NN that_WDT occurs_VVZ upstream_RB of_IN a_DT ship_NN bow_NN have_VHP not_RB been_VBN found_VVN in_IN the_DT literature_NN ,_, and_CC most_JJS of_IN the_DT studies_NNS were_VBD focused_VVN on_IN the_DT impact_NN pressure_NN of_IN the_DT wave_NN ._SENT 
Instead_RB ,_, similar_JJ phenomena_NNS ,_, which_WDT have_VHP an_DT almost_RB identical_JJ behaviour_NN as_IN spray_NN cloud_NN formation_NN ,_, have_VHP been_VBN reported_VVN and_CC analyzed_VVN ._SENT 
It_PP is_VBZ clear_JJ that_IN the_DT full_JJ direct_JJ numerical_JJ simulation_NN of_IN wave-ship_NN interaction_NN for_IN the_DT generation_NN of_IN spray_NN clouds_NNS is_VBZ not_RB a_DT viable_JJ option_NN at_IN this_DT time_NN ,_, but_CC the_DT stages_NNS of_IN this_DT process_NN can_MD be_VB modeled_VVN separately_RB ._SENT 
However_RB ,_, even_RB these_DT separate_JJ process_NN involved_VVN in_IN spray_NN cloud_NN formation_NN need_VVP to_TO be_VB further_RBR developed_VVN ._SENT 
Even_RB predicting_VVG and_CC modeling_VVG wave_NN slamming_VVG behaviour_NN with_IN the_DT bow_NN is_VBZ a_DT complex_JJ problem_NN ._SENT 
Phenomena_NNS ,_, such_JJ as_IN air_NN entrainment_NN ,_, compressibility_NN effects_NNS ,_, and_CC predicting_VVG full_JJ scale_NN values_NNS from_IN scaled_VVN experiments_NNS remain_VVP to_TO be_VB better_RBR developed_VVN ._SENT 
The_DT experimental_JJ and/or_JJ numerical_JJ methods_NNS associated_VVN with_IN the_DT particular_JJ parts_NNS of_IN the_DT process_NN ,_, such_JJ as_IN wave-slamming_NP ,_, free_JJ surface_NN capturing_VVG ,_, air_NN entrainment_NN ,_, turbulence_NN models_NNS ,_, and_CC droplet_NN breakup_NN are_VBP covered_VVN in_IN the_DT remaining_VVG sections_NNS of_IN the_DT review_NN ._SENT 
Some_DT of_IN these_DT individual_JJ phenomena_NNS have_VHP specific_JJ solutions_NNS and_CC corresponding_JJ lab_NN experiments_NNS ,_, but_CC some_DT were_VBD reviewed_VVN because_IN of_IN the_DT similarity_NN of_IN the_DT solutions_NNS ._SENT 
These_DT similar_JJ methods_NNS and_CC studies_NNS are_VBP suggested_VVN for_IN adaptation_NN to_TO the_DT present_JJ problem_NN ._SENT 
The_DT future_NN of_IN numerical_JJ prediction_NN in_IN this_DT field_NN is_VBZ in_IN CFD_NN ._SENT 
However_RB ,_, the_DT multi-scale_JJ nature_NN of_IN this_DT problem_NN makes_VVZ calculation_NN computationally_RB expensive_JJ ._SENT 
The_DT power_NN and_CC memory_NN capability_NN of_IN new_JJ multi-processor_NN computers_NNS makes_VVZ modeling_VVG the_DT phenomena_NNS possible_JJ ;_: however_RB ,_, it_PP takes_VVZ days_NNS to_TO simulate_VV the_DT prediction_NN of_IN wave_NN slamming_VVG incidents_NNS ,_, droplet_NN breakup_NN ,_, and_CC a_DT turbulence_NN model_NN with_IN small_JJ computational_JJ cells_NNS in_IN the_DT domain_NN ._SENT 
The_DT recent_JJ numerical_JJ prediction_NN method_NN ,_, SPH_NN is_VBZ becoming_VVG more_RBR popular_JJ and_CC is_VBZ a_DT robust_JJ method_NN for_IN prediction_NN of_IN the_DT body-fluid_JJ interface_NN ,_, which_WDT can_MD be_VB used_VVN together_RB with_IN classic_JJ CFD_NN methods_NNS to_TO produce_VV cost-efficient_JJ and_CC accurate_JJ modeling_NN for_IN the_DT interaction_NN and_CC spray_NN generation_NN phenomenon_NN ._SENT 
This_DT study_NN shows_VVZ the_DT current_JJ trends_NNS in_IN modeling_VVG and_CC analyzing_VVG spray_NN cloud_NN formation_NN arising_VVG from_IN wave_NN impact_NN with_IN objects_NNS at_IN the_DT sea_NN surface_NN in_IN cold_JJ regions_NNS ,_, which_WDT leads_VVZ to_TO icing_VVG on_IN vessels_NNS and_CC offshore_JJ structures_NNS ._SENT 
In_IN order_NN to_TO better_RBR understand_VV these_DT phenomena_NNS ,_, the_DT best_JJS approach_NN at_IN present_NN is_VBZ numerical_JJ and_CC experimental_JJ studies_NNS of_IN the_DT separate_JJ stages_NNS of_IN the_DT processes_NNS ,_, which_WDT should_MD be_VB verified_VVN and_CC compared_VVN with_IN field_NN observation_NN data_NNS ._SENT 
The_DT influence_NN of_IN all_PDT the_DT identified_VVN parameters_NNS on_IN spray_NN cloud_NN formation_NN are_VBP still_RB poorly_RB understood_VVN ._SENT 
More_RBR precise_JJ considerations_NNS will_MD be_VB needed_VVN in_IN studying_VVG each_DT of_IN these_DT parts_NNS ,_, which_WDT can_MD then_RB be_VB built_VVN into_IN an_DT overall_JJ model_NN ._SENT 
The_DT present_JJ gaps_NNS in_IN this_DT field_NN have_VHP been_VBN highlighted_VVN ,_, and_CC appropriate_JJ methods_NNS and_CC solutions_NNS for_IN future_JJ study_NN were_VBD suggested_VVN for_IN each_DT stage_NN of_IN the_DT process_NN ._SENT
